  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_605610a3-6095-4d3c-baf6-874da0cae5dd'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

  <span id="freeText13153161899927894742" style="display:none">Early in her life, Josephine Malone learned the hard way that there was only one person she could love and trust: her grandmother, Lydia Malone. Out of necessity, unconsciously and very successfully, Josephine donned a disguise to keep all others at bay. She led a globetrotting lifestyle on the fringes of the fashion and music elite, but she kept herself distant. <br /> <br />While Josephine was trotting the globe, retired boxer Jake Spear was living in the same small town as Lydia. There was nothing disguised about Jake. Including the fact he made a habit of making very bad decisions about who to give his love. <br /> <br />But for Josephine and Jake, there was one person who adored them. One person who knew how to lead them to happiness. And one person who was intent on doing it. <br /> <br />Even if she had to do it as her final wish on this earth. <br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17668141067291854179"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395769849i/9042777._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392435ra/755438.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>**** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED **** <b> 5++ STARS!! </b><br/><br/><strong>W-O-W!!! This book was <u>EPIC</u>. Absolutely PERFECT!!! </strong><br/><br/>Before anything else, I just want to say that if you're already a Kristen Ashley fan, you'll understand when I say that this book is <em>
  <strong>"Vintage KA" </strong>
</em>style -- PURE GOLD!!! And, if you've never read a KA book before, this would be an awesome book to start with!! It's a <em></em><u>standalone</u> romance and is since it's so fantabulous, it would be a wonderful introduction to this author's amazing books :)<br/><br/>A few thing</span>
  <span id="freeText17668141067291854179" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395769849i/9042777._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392435ra/755438.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>**** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED **** <b> 5++ STARS!! </b><br><br><strong>W-O-W!!! This book was <u>EPIC</u>. Absolutely PERFECT!!! </strong><br><br>Before anything else, I just want to say that if you're already a Kristen Ashley fan, you'll understand when I say that this book is <em>
  <strong>"Vintage KA" </strong>
</em>style -- PURE GOLD!!! And, if you've never read a KA book before, this would be an awesome book to start with!! It's a <em></em><u>standalone</u> romance and is since it's so fantabulous, it would be a wonderful introduction to this author's amazing books :)<br><br>A few things right off the bat....<br><br>✦ This might honestly be my favorite KA book. Or, gah, that's like choosing a favorite child, but it's definitely one of them. And without a doubt Jake and Josie are one of my favorite KA couples. This is coming from the perspective of someone who has read nearly every single book KA has written too!<br><br>✦ This book is <em>looooong!!! </em>It was 9568 "locations" on my Kindle and every single word in them was brilliant!! I am <em>so</em> happy that it wasn't edited down!<br><br>✦ EPIC FEELS. This book has them. In bucket loads. From the very first page to the gorgeous, heartfelt, tear-enducing epilogue at the end, this book <em>made me</em> <em>feel. </em><br><br>✦ This is worth mentioning again: <u>
  <strong>VINTAGE KA</strong>
</u>, guys. 'Nuff said <strong>♥</strong><br><br> <br><br>Ok... on to the real review...<br><br>The pure joy felt when opening up a new KA book is just exhilarating. You just <em>know</em> that you're in for a wild ride filled with fantastic writing, Alpha males, and sexy romance... and this book had it <em>all!!</em><br><br>Kristen Ashley truly is one of the most talented authors I've read. In my eyes, no one writes like her, and I really mean <em>no one</em>. If you've read her books, you know what I mean. Her <em>descriptions</em> and just the <em>way</em> she writes is so unique to her that it's almost like she has her own language. If you were to give me ten random paragraphs of writing from various authors, I'd be able to pick out which one she wrote in a heartbeat. You <em>feel</em> it so strongly. Every word just sinks into your heart and soul.<br><br>Less than two pages into this book and I already had <em>shivers</em> running through me and my heart was racing. There was this moment right at the beginning where their eyes meet across the cemetery and I didn't even know the characters yet but the <em>feels</em> just hit <em>so</em> strongly and I was <em>hooked</em>!!!<br><br>The story takes place in the town of Magdalene where Josie returns for the funeral of her beloved grandmother. Her work takes her traveling all over the world but her grandmother was everything to her and she takes some time off to come back and stay at her house after. When she goes in for the reading of the will, she find that her grandmother put into motion a very unusual request which brings Jake Spear into her life in a way she never expected.... and so begins one of the <em>very best</em> romances I have ever read <strong>♥</strong><br><br>I love all kinds of romance but lets be honest, a lot of them are about couples between 18-35 and I loved that this one was about a couple in their 40s. Jake actually had three kids (PS -- I <em>adored</em> them) and both him and Josie had a certain... stability (?) and no-nonsense attitude to their characters that I guess came with simply having made a lot of mistakes in their lives and (more importantly) having learned from them. I loved that this book basically acknowledged that not everyone finds their forever love early on and what it also meant was that having lived without it for so long, both Jake and Josie valued it so highly when they got it, they both knew how precious what they had was and <em>that</em> was just beautiful.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"Never keep anything from me, I don't give a shit how you think I'm gonna react. I'll react how I react. I will NEVER harm you doin' it. But I got enough experience with what doesn't work between a man and a woman to know that keeping' shit from each other is a big fuckin' part of that….. Every inch of you, outside and any way you can get inside, baby, physically or emotionally, is mine."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>My heart felt <em>full</em> to bursting throughout the whole time I was reading this. There's just no other way to describe it. I was just so <em>with</em> the story that like the randomest little things would make me tear up (even if they weren't sad) just becauseI was <em>feeling</em> so much.<br><br>I love love <em>loved</em> Jake. Talk about ALPHA!!! He  was bossy but in a loveable way with a total take-no-bullshit attitude. And yes, a few of you know already that he was a boxer but guys, he was <em>so </em>much more than that too. He had so many sides to him, so many roles, so many talents ( *winks* ) .... he was a great father and a gorgeous lover and yes, he was also one heckuva badass fighter, but at the end of the day, he was just a wonderful guy who cared for his loved ones more than anything else in the world and was willing to go to any lengths to bring them safety and happiness. He stole my heart.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"You good?" he asked into the top of my hair.</em>
    <br>
    <br>
    <em>I stared at the shadowed wall of his chest.</em>
    <br>
    <br>
    <em>"Josie?" he called when I didn't answer.</em>
    <br>
    <br>
    <em>"I'm afraid," I admitted softly.</em>
    <br>
    <br>
    <em>His arms pulled me closer and I felt his lips on my hair when he answered, "Beat that back, honey. No reason to be scared. Not with me."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Josephine was all kinds of cool!! She was... gah, it's hard to explain... she was a hoot! Very proper and she spoke in a very cultured manner -- and by that I mean that words like <em>illuminating, alas, distressing, prowess, vociferous, fibbed, ungentlemanly, await, hence, irksome, </em>and more were all part of her regular vocabulary. But while she had this very collected side to her, she also had the biggest heart and had such a beautiful personality. She was feisty and smart and fun and I loved the way she cared so deeply not only for Jake but also for his children. She was just awesome!!<br><br>And the dynamic of the two of them playing off each other was pure gold!!! With her being so proper and him being so chill... they were so different but yet they just fit <em>perfectly</em> together. It was brilliant!!!!!!<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"What's next?" I queried.</em>
    <br>
    <br>
    <em>"Don't know, Josie. Just know whatever it is I want you to be a part of it and I hope like fuck you want the same."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br><br>What I loved about them most though was how no matter what life threw at them, they didn't let themselves get dragged down the wrong path. There was just a refreshing lack of 'stupidity' from either of them in this book. Don't laugh, you know what I mean. Gosh, it was just such an <em>amazing</em> feeling to genuinely have that heartfelt <em>respect</em> for the characters. I not only liked them both as people but also agreed with and understood their decisions and the way they handled their lives, families, and relationships. They had each others' back, supported each other, and didn't let anything bring them down.<br><br>This book was one gorgeous, <em>epic</em> moment after another. I read so many scenes literally clutching at my heart or squeeing out loud with the hugest grin you can imagine on my face. I not only have whole paragraphs of text highlighted text but there are a few sections where I highlighted several pages on end.<br><br>Also, while Kristen Ashley is well known for her Alpha male characters, another thing that many of her fans will eagerly agree to is that she writes magical epilogues and I can say with full certainty that this was one of the most heartfelt, emotional, and deeply powerful epilogues she's ever written. Tears were pouring down my face. It was just so beautiful!!<br><br>On a bit of a random note, I think was makes KA's alphas so amazing is that they each perfectly ride that balance between dominant, possessive, caring, and badass -- they're family men, fighters, protectors, lovers, friends, everything. Some are a little 'safer', some are a little 'edgier', some more dangerous, others more swoony ... and each one of them has a slightly different mix of all these qualities that makes them unique. They each ride that line between almost <em>too much</em> and just absolutely <em>right</em>. It's like, they're extreme enough to make your heart race but they feel just real enough to make you accept them. They're not perfect people though, they have all kinds of flaws and vices and often even make us mad but we love them as they are. They really are the perfect Alpha males.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"To have what Jake had you had to be born the man he became. You couldn't want it. You simply were going to be it until you were it."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br><br><br><br><em>The Will</em> is one of the most beautifully written and genuinely heart warming romances I have ever read. This is the kind of book you can lose yourself in. It had everything we have come to <em>love </em>from VintageKA -- a loooooooong story, oodles of details, phenomenal dialogue, family dynamics unlike any other, hot &amp; passionate romance and that special and totally unique language style that carries the weight, meaning, and heartfelt power that only a Kristen Ashley book can ever deliver.<br><br>This book was perfection. I do not have a single complaint. Quite simply, this was KA at her best!!<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>“I never wanted anything but you, Jake… And I wanted you before I even knew you… You’re everything I ever wanted, darling.”</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br><br><strong>Rating: 5+++ STARS!!!</strong><br><br>****************************<br><br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="17668141067291854179" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              >

  <br/>
  <a href='http://amzn.to/1B91I63' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon CA</a>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424794765i/13803175._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo e9f39846-8657-4625-87ca-96d7890859e4_zps4f07e6e1.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><b><u>April 3, 2014</u><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396535676i/9148528.jpg' alt=' photo 0993176d-633b-458a-a560-c79504bd8161_zps4f605355.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>If ever there was a book that conveyed this message perfectly, this is the one.<br/><br/><br/>*** Thank you to 'TheSubClubBooks' and Kristen Ashley for providing me with an ARC of this book for review. <br/><br/>(My review of "The Will" for The Sub Club Books <a href='http://thesubclubbooks.com/?p=21578' rel='nofollow noopener'>HERE</a> and below.)<br/><br/><br/><i>“Why I love Kristen Ashley” by Irene<br/> <br/>I started reading Kristen Ashley a few years </i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText16509925108090475420" style="display:none"><br>This KA goodness is currently on sale for ONLY .99 <br>(or a buck and a quarter if you are in Canada ;) LOL!)<br><br><b>
  <a href="http://amzn.to/1A3vCmI" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon US</a>
  <br>
  <br>
  <a href="http://amzn.to/1w7QPLR" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon UK</a>
  <br>
  <br>
  <a href="http://amzn.to/1B91I63" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon CA</a>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424794765i/13803175._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo e9f39846-8657-4625-87ca-96d7890859e4_zps4f07e6e1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><br><b><u>April 3, 2014</u><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396535676i/9148528.jpg" alt=" photo 0993176d-633b-458a-a560-c79504bd8161_zps4f605355.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If ever there was a book that conveyed this message perfectly, this is the one.<br><br><br>*** Thank you to 'TheSubClubBooks' and Kristen Ashley for providing me with an ARC of this book for review. <br><br>(My review of "The Will" for The Sub Club Books <a href="http://thesubclubbooks.com/?p=21578" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE</a> and below.)<br><br><br><i>“Why I love Kristen Ashley” by Irene<br> <br>I started reading Kristen Ashley a few years ago. It all started with her “Dream Man” series, followed by “Rock Chick” series, then “Colorado Mountain” and finally “The ‘Burg”. The last two have remained my favorite series and “The ‘Burg” produced Joe Callahan, who proudly holds the title of “KA’s Ultimate Alpha” in my eyes. After having met Jake from “The Will”, I considered [several times!] stripping Joe of that title and handing it over to Jake. If you who know me and my devotion to Joe, that should tell you something about Jake and “The Will”.<br> <br>What I love about Kirsten’s books is that they always make me feel. Be it happy, sad, angry, etc. the feels are always present and that’s one of the reasons I always look forward to Ms Ashley’s new releases.<br> <br>One of the other reasons I enjoy her books is the message they tend to convey. Some of my favorite ones include “not everyone is perfect but that’s OK” and “life doesn’t end after 40″. If you are like me (in your 40s and love Kristen’s work), you’d know what I am talking about when I say her books to me now what John Hughes movies were to me back when I was growing up. You can relate to her characters because they deal with stuff most of us deal on a daily bases (moody kids, relationship issues, juggling work and home life, etc.) and they are ‘perfectly flawed’ (as I like to call them) because, let’s face it, perfection is boring!<br> <br>“The Will” delivered all of the above and then some! Even though the series itself is new, it was good old Kristen doing what she does best! To say she knocked this one out of the ballpark would be an understatement! This book is an absolute perfection, as far as I am concerned. I tried (not that I look for it in a book but you know what I mean) to find something to complain about but couldn’t come up with one single thing! <br><br>We got an outstanding supporting cast that hopefully has a guy in it that will be the subject of the next book in the series, Mickey (crossing fingers and toes!!! Pleeeeeease, Kristen!!!). We got Gran who is the world of wisdom and ever present even though she isn’t (if that makes sense). We got one of the most adorable child characters ever written, Ethan. There is even a town douche (because every books needs one!) and an awesome BFF (or two) to take our sweet Josie’s back. <br><br>And then, of course, there is Jake … super daddy, ex-boxer, great friend and, last but absolutely NOT least, a SUPER Alpha, that ‘rough around the edges’ type of hero that we’ve grown to know and love, the kind that only Kristen can deliver.<br> <br>The journey of Jake and Josie that Ms. Ashley takes us on is an emotional one but it’s worth every tear, happy and sad. And then, just when you thought this book couldn’t get any better, the woman delivers one of those awesome epilogues she is known for so don’t put that Kleenex box away just yet …<br> <br>I am not going to talk about sex because, if you are familiar with Kristen’s men, you’d know that very few characaters do it better.<br> <br>I’ve said it before in one of my earlier reviews of Kristen’s work but I am happy to repeat myself: I hope Kristen Ashley never stops writing because, if she does, I might have to stop reading.<br> <br>Final verdict: 5+ glorious, knock out stars indeed ;)<br><br>P.S. Just in case you were wondering, Joe is still my #1 but Jake is now a VERY close second … </i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396996983i/9216274.jpg" alt=" photo 4ce5566c-debd-47d7-93ae-f9051756d55c_zps63e4d9df.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><u>Favorite quote</u>: <i>"It hit him in that moment in a way he knew he'd never forget that he could take that hand and she could lead him anywhere."</i><br><br><u>Favorite character (aside from Jake)</u>: Ethan.<br><br><u>Favorite part</u>: Jake &amp; Josie's very first sexual encounter.<br><br><br>Re: epilogue - even though it wasn't my favorite of her epilogues, it was still really sweet and made me shed a tear (or two).<br><br><br>Cheers for now! <br><br><br>P.S. Join us for a BR of 'The Will' <b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/topic/show/1762210-the-will-buddy-read-4-8-14" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE</a></b> on April 8, 2014.<br><br>P.P.S. My absolute FAVORITE review of this book: <b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/889941192" rel="nofollow noopener">Wendy's review of 'The Will'</a></b>. Talk about hitting the nail on the head! </b></span>

<div id="review_826202435" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/826202435" />
    <a title="Mo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11856352-mo"><img alt="Mo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1371247812p2/11856352.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/826202435?book_show_action=true">Jan 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mo" href="/user/show/11856352-mo">Mo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer826202435" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5579746972358599049">It behoves me to write a review about this delectable novel. Perchance, bear with me, as I therefore strive to put into words my thoughts and feelings about dearest Josephine and Jake. Indeed it was an experience that alas had to end.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>His black hair had a hint of silvery-gray in it. It was thick and clipped well but in a way that was not a nod to style, instead it was apparent he didn’t want to spend time on it so his style was wash and go.</b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397044618i/9223189._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>This morning he had not shaved and he had a dark s</b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText5579746972358599049" style="display:none">It behoves me to write a review about this delectable novel. Perchance, bear with me, as I therefore strive to put into words my thoughts and feelings about dearest Josephine and Jake. Indeed it was an experience that alas had to end.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>His black hair had a hint of silvery-gray in it. It was thick and clipped well but in a way that was not a nod to style, instead it was apparent he didn’t want to spend time on it so his style was wash and go.</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397044618i/9223189._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>This morning he had not shaved and he had a dark shadow of black and silver stubble on his jaw.</b>
</blockquote><br><br>I have been a fan of KA for a number of years now. Sweet Dreams is one of my favourite books ever. Tate Jackson is my number one hero. I know a few of us bemoaned the fact that Kristen took up with a Publisher and some of those books that she released through said publisher were not really what we wanted. So when I heard this one was self-published, I was very happy, very happy indeed.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397044618i/9223190._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Josie Malone returns to Magdalene for the reading of her Grandmother’s will, hence the title, my dear friends. Her Grandmother has left a strange request in her will. At the reading of the will she meets Jake Spear. They don’t exactly hit it off in the beginning.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>”Fuckin’ hell, you ever show Lydie how far that stick was shoved up your ass?”<br><br>Well!<br>I never!</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397044618ra/9223191.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Lets just state that Josie does talk like she has a stick up her ass. In the beginning it really annoyed me. I mean who speaks like a Victorian maiden in the 21st Century. I felt I was back in Pemberly or Downton Abbey. But I got over myself and eventually ended up loving her.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397044618i/9223192._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>”DO NOT FUCKIN’ TELL ME WHAT MY LANGUAGE IS.”</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Jake (swoon), is your typical alpha KA hero. He is brash, he is crude, he uses bad language, his form of employment isn’t exactly the best. But I loved him. Did he topple Tate or Joe from number one spot? Nope, but nearly, very nearly indeed.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397044618i/9223193.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>”Maybe it has somethin’ to do with you bein’ a judgmental, stick up your ass bitch who’d react just the way you reacted about a minute ago if she told you about me.”</b>
</blockquote><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397040934ra/9222672.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>They eventually do come round and end up liking each other. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>”You crack me right the fuck up, babe.”</b>
</blockquote><br><br>I won’t say too much as you are better off just discovering the beauty of a KA novel all by yourself.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397041534i/9222723._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>The area between my legs was pulsing.<br>My focus was riveted.<br>I was gone.</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423646935i/13653787.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Josie is very prim and proper and I was so looking forward to her getting her knickers in a twist (and her getting her knickers off, I might add) and it was definitely worth the wait for that to happen.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>”Wish like fuck I could strip you bare and fuck you on my couch right about now.”</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Loved Jake and his dirty talk.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397044618i/9223198._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><blockquote>
  <b>Thus, his fingers were not smooth … Thus, his fingers were calloused and abrasive</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396976775i/9212997._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>”You can pay for my assistance in orgasms.”</b>
</blockquote><br>Yeah, Josie did lighten up a bit.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397044618i/9223196._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>”You got one choice, you either suck me or I eat you. After that, I take over.”</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397044618i/9223197._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And I loved his kids. Normal kids.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>I’ll love you always…</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397044618i/9223199._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And as for the ending and the epilogue… OMG, you will definitely shed a tear. I know I did.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397045038i/9223220.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Thanks to Irene for making sure this was on our radar for release date and the Canaries for the BR - sorry I ran ahead of you all. xxx</span>
  <a data-text-id="5579746972358599049" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_803307032" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/803307032" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/803307032?book_show_action=true">Dec 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781311349538" href="/book/show/20332278-the-will">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer803307032" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5657093907253626673"><b>5 Lavender stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/e5ec3728-6c07-4cd9-acb0-a0a1dd85f4ab_zps621bfc99.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397208038i/9247019.jpg' alt=' photo e5ec3728-6c07-4cd9-acb0-a0a1dd85f4ab_zps621bfc99.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>When I started seeing early reviews for <i>The Will</i>, I just knew it was going to be good. When it was compared to some of Kristen Ashley’s older stuff, I got all excited. This was a long book (perfect) and extremely descriptive (I love), not at all rushed and just gave me that feeling I get when I read a crazy good KA read. I am such a fan of hers. If someone told me I could only read books by one author ever again, I wouldn’t hesitate to answer. Kristen Ashley. That’s how much</span>
  <span id="freeText5657093907253626673" style="display:none"><b>5 Lavender stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/e5ec3728-6c07-4cd9-acb0-a0a1dd85f4ab_zps621bfc99.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397208038i/9247019.jpg" alt=" photo e5ec3728-6c07-4cd9-acb0-a0a1dd85f4ab_zps621bfc99.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>When I started seeing early reviews for <i>The Will</i>, I just knew it was going to be good. When it was compared to some of Kristen Ashley’s older stuff, I got all excited. This was a long book (perfect) and extremely descriptive (I love), not at all rushed and just gave me that feeling I get when I read a crazy good KA read. I am such a fan of hers. If someone told me I could only read books by one author ever again, I wouldn’t hesitate to answer. Kristen Ashley. That’s how much I love her stuff. This book was the best book she’s had out recently. A truly beautiful story.<br><br>Josephine Malone is used to being alone. She lives a life on the go, traveling with her boss of 23 years who is a famous photographer. She enjoys her life. She has her Gran and her boss/friend Henry. She is content with that. With being alone. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/194331ac-b8bc-4d8d-9f5d-42d5f33c4c65_zpsfbd53e80.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397208038i/9247020.jpg" alt=" photo 194331ac-b8bc-4d8d-9f5d-42d5f33c4c65_zpsfbd53e80.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Josie’s Gran was the only good thing about her childhood. This is the reason she’s never let many people in. Her Gran never wanted that life for her. She wanted her to be with someone special. Someone who would love her passionately and always be there for her. Gran wanted her with Jake Spears. <br><br>Jake and Josie first see each other at the funeral of her Gran. He is there with his three children. Jake Spear hasn’t had an easy go either. He’s been in failed marriage after failed marriage. He has three beautiful children to show for them, but he’s never been able to pick the right girl. Josie’s Gran had been a godsend for him. As an ex-fighter struggling with his gym, Gran was able to help him, not only with that, but with his children. Gran was somthing special to the Spear bunch, just as she was to Josie. <br><br>When Josie goes to the reading of her Gran’s will, there is one other person there. Jake Spear.<br><i>
  <blockquote>“My most precious possession, the thing I treasure about anything else in this world, that being my granddaughter, Josephine Diana Malone, I hereby bequeath to James Markham Spear.”</blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/153a28cc-261c-48d3-a60d-4acba7dc1eb6_zps7449bfbb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397208038i/9247021.jpg" alt=" photo 153a28cc-261c-48d3-a60d-4acba7dc1eb6_zps7449bfbb.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> Josie is thrown for a loop. Gran never mentioned this Jake. And she wants them to what, be together? in what complicity? <br><i>
  <blockquote>“I don’t understand what Gran wanted for you and me.”<br><br> “Maybe she wanted us to be friends? Maybe she wanted to know you got someone who cares, who’ll look out for you, listen to you, take your back when you need it and give a shit not just when you need it but all the time.”</blockquote>
</i><br>Although she is hesitant at first, Josie decides to give Jake a chance. For her Gran. Josie gets to know Jake, gets to know his children. Starts to look at her life differently. Maybe it wouldn’t be so bad to stay at the Lavender House. Set down some roots. <br><br>At first, I wasn’t so sure about Josie. She was so prim and proper, seemed to be judgmental etc. After some time, I started to love her. She is an amazing heroine. Although she talks like a proper lady, she isn’t completely stuck up. She is full of love, and she’s caring and compassionate. She’s klutzy and funny. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“You are not a fool,” he whispered. “You can never be a fool. You’re total class from top to toe. You’re also a klutz. Own that, baby, because it’s cute and because it’s you. If you learn to accept yourself just as you are, learn to laugh at your quirks instead of hating them, show the world all that’s you without tryin’ to hide things that are not even a little unattractive, that makes you more attractive. What you got is a fuckuva lot. You own all of it and let it all hang out, you’ll go off-the-charts.” </blockquote>
</i><br>As Jake and Josie’s friendship develops, they both start to see what Gran wanted for them. Why she picked them for one another. Two completely different people from totally different worlds might just be the perfect match.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/46bc424b-c1d4-4e27-96e1-6bb766645724_zps9d566c65.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397208038i/9247022.jpg" alt=" photo 46bc424b-c1d4-4e27-96e1-6bb766645724_zps9d566c65.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“We have each other now.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> Jake Spear stole my heart. He may be a strip club owner with three children and just as many ex-wives, but he was perfection. An ex-fighter, rough around the edges with the most fiercely protective and gentle heart. He was an amazing and devoted father. He was sweet, possessive and incredibly sexy. The perfect KA alpha. I loved how he was with Josie. He knew how to treat her, how to handle her. And watching Josie with his kids made me melt. You wouldn’t think she would be good with them, being this proper lady who’s never had children, but she was exactly what the Spear family needed. Maybe, just maybe Gran was on to something. Maybe this is the chance for true love and happiness both Jake and Josie have been waiting for.<br><i>
  <blockquote>“Thank you for taking care of me, darling.”<br> “My job, baby.” he replied.<br><br>“I’m glad your good at it.” </blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/8ebb6b13-46be-476f-a6be-95b8139e4602_zpsc3ac9a21.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397208038i/9247023.jpg" alt=" photo 8ebb6b13-46be-476f-a6be-95b8139e4602_zpsc3ac9a21.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>The Will</i> is a beautiful, heart warming story about love, loss, family, friendship and showing that it’s never ever too late to believe in love. This book... Ah this book. It made my heart happy. I fell in love with Jake, Josie, Connor, Amber, Ethan, even boy Taylor and girl Taylor. And lets not forget the writing. Kristen Ashley knows how to write a book. Even though this was a very long book (twice the length of the average book I read), it didn’t feel that way. I never wanted it to end. I was moved to tears more than once, especially towards the end. That epilogue was just epic. I feel like I could go on and on and on about how wonderful this was and how much I loved it, but I think you get the hint. For all you KA lovers, this is one you won’t want to miss out on! <br><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/c163f3ee-999a-4486-9339-2db8f92980d3_zpsae99a7e0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397208038i/9247024.jpg" alt=" photo c163f3ee-999a-4486-9339-2db8f92980d3_zpsae99a7e0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>Forever and Completely. </blockquote>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="5657093907253626673" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish"><img alt="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1398981306p2/1113032.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/826437164?book_show_action=true">Jan 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="user" itemprop="url" name="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish">UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781311349538" href="/book/show/20332278-the-will">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=first-in-series-trilogy-duet">first-in-series-trilogy-duet</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=abuse-physical-emotional-sexual">abuse-physical-emotional-sexual</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=teen-angst">teen-angst</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer826437164" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12113073659421439151"><br/>People are calling this 'old school Kristen Ashley storytelling', and I agree. That's why I'm giving it...<br/><br/><b>...5 bright, passionate, sigh-worthy stars</b><br/><br/><i>“It hit him in that moment in a way he knew he’d never forget that he could take that hand and she could lead him anywhere. Just tip up her lips, turn those eyes to him and hold out her hand and he’d go straight to hell with her and do it smiling.”</i><br/><br/><i>
  <b>Such a fun, romantic, sexy story!</b>
</i><br/><br/>It will come as no surprise to anyone that I’m a huge fan of Kriste</span>
  <span id="freeText12113073659421439151" style="display:none"><br />People are calling this 'old school Kristen Ashley storytelling', and I agree. That's why I'm giving it...<br /><br /><b>...5 bright, passionate, sigh-worthy stars</b><br /><br /><i>“It hit him in that moment in a way he knew he’d never forget that he could take that hand and she could lead him anywhere. Just tip up her lips, turn those eyes to him and hold out her hand and he’d go straight to hell with her and do it smiling.”</i><br /><br /><i>
  <b>Such a fun, romantic, sexy story!</b>
</i><br /><br />It will come as no surprise to anyone that I’m a huge fan of Kristen Ashley’s writing, and it’s stories like <i>The Will</i> that, book after book, keep me coming back for more. This first in the new <i>Magdalene</i> series has that awesome small town setting we’ve come to love in her stories, and the coastal town of Magdalene introduces us to some fantastic characters with amazing stories to tell! <br /><br /><b>Description…</b><blockquote>Early in her life, Josephine Malone learned the hard way that there was only one person she could love and trust: her grandmother, Lydia Malone. Out of necessity, unconsciously and very successfully, Josephine donned a disguise to keep all others at bay. She led a globetrotting lifestyle on the fringes of the fashion and music elite, but she kept herself distant.<br /><br />While Josephine was trotting the globe, retired boxer Jake Spear was living in the same small town as Lydia. There was nothing disguised about Jake. Including the fact he made a habit of making very bad decisions about who to give his love.<br /><br />But for Josephine and Jake, there was one person who adored them. One person who knew how to lead them to happiness. And one person who was intent on doing it.<br /><br />Even if she had to do it as her final wish on this earth.</blockquote><b>My thoughts…</b><br /><br />Gotta say, I really am excited about this series. The town with its residents who have the same hopes and dreams, the same trials and triumphs as the rest of us, is a place I would love to call home, with people I’d love to call friends. <br /><br />Josie is a woman I didn’t connect with right away. She was so aloof, so standoffish, holding herself apart from the world around her. The way she talked, the way she dressed, the way she carried herself… everything about her said, <i>back off!</i> But when she finally got her chance to shine, her shine was like a million bright, blinding lights, and that's when she won me over, heart and soul. This woman who stepped up and loved and, holding nothing back, loved in a way she would change lives... yes… heart and soul, she had me.<br /><br />Jake. Wow. Just <i>wow!</i> What a great hero he is! A man who put his heart out there, time and time again, until he felt he had nothing left of his heart to give. A man devoted to his children. A man determined to take care of his own, and do it in his own way. I fell for Jake hard, and did it early on. Giving, caring, funny, accepting, and hell yeah, all kinds of sexy. Jake is a man to be respected, feared, but most of all, he’s a man to be loved.<br /><br />And, as she always does, Kristen Ashley has created this world and filled it with amazing people. The supporting cast is made up of men and women whose stories need to be told, and I’ve no doubt each and every one will be amazing!<br /><br /><b>The bottom line…</b><br /><br />What’s left to say? I love this new world filled with unending possibilities and can’t wait to see where Kristen Ashley takes us next!<br /><br /><i>My thanks to Kristen Ashley for providing me with a copy of this story in exchange for an honest review. As always, it has been such a treat!</i><br /><br />If you're already a Kristen Ashley addict, or interested in checking out her books, be sure to stop by our <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/66492.Kristen_Ashley_Addict_s_Support_Group" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley Addict's Support Group</a> here on Goodreads!</span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_889941192" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/889941192" />
    <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts"><img alt="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1378340325p2/17755575.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/889941192?book_show_action=true">Mar 23, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts">Wendy&#39;sThoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781311349538" href="/book/show/20332278-the-will">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">KA Fans, Romance, Everyone</span></div>

        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer889941192" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8764314817217958704"><b>5 Pulled an All-Nighter, Breaking the Facade, Letting Love in Stars<br/>* * * * *<i>Spoiler Free</i><br/>This book knocked me to my mental knees...There were so many things to address, trying to come up with a way to present them all caused my head to spin.<br/><br/>First... the reader would either be able to connect with the main character Josie... or not. KA was fearless in her determination to stay true to what she felt this woman needed to be. This was a huge risk and for some readers, it may have been too much of a l</b></span>
  <span id="freeText8764314817217958704" style="display:none"><b>5 Pulled an All-Nighter, Breaking the Facade, Letting Love in Stars<br>* * * * *<i>Spoiler Free</i><br>This book knocked me to my mental knees...There were so many things to address, trying to come up with a way to present them all caused my head to spin.<br><br>First... the reader would either be able to connect with the main character Josie... or not. KA was fearless in her determination to stay true to what she felt this woman needed to be. This was a huge risk and for some readers, it may have been too much of a leap of faith for them... they had experienced recent books by her which for some reason or another were not totally true to the KA voice as they knew it...so to be hit from the first page by a fully formed character such as Josie could be a deal-breaker. <br><br>I get that... and to those who felt "Eh, WTH...", I understand and get that, too... no harm/no foul... and on to the next book...<br><br>But for me... I got something besides that...I sensed a whole undercurrent brewing and was hooked from the start... because... <br><br>From my life perspective, I have come to believe no matter where you live, what you believe politically or socially, whether you identify yourself as Blue or White Collar, Elite, Independent or Recluse... the driving force in life is to love and be loved.</b> This statement may be very simplistic yet when we attempt to find it with others..... it can remain elusive.<br><br>Our lives are these lessons; whether we have them forced upon us brutally.... or learn them from more gentle teachers... we always remember them, and they can skew our understanding of this powerful force ... love... and learn to hide from it.<br><br>Which brings me to Josie... Her developmental stages were riddled with lies, betrayal, fear, abandonment, and pain. These were the major lessons she learned from parents who were supposed to love her unconditionally. Instead, she saw with her young eyes the horrors of inflicted pain by her father; she survived to her teenage years by learning to hide anything which might give her happiness. She then paid the price of feeling happiness by physical pain at the hands of her father when he found out she had experienced anything without his approval. It was so severe she was hospitalized. This allowed her gran, Lydia to step in and remove her without any resistance from her father.<br><br>Her Gran was her only safe haven. What was critical for Josie was her understanding of her Gran's own history of abuse and how she survived; this was a family steeped in it for generations. It had left its mark and her Gran had risen above it...so she was able to give the guidance Josie needed growing up. She enrolled Josie into a prestigious all-girls school which gave her education, literature, and friendship. It also was the type of place which exposed her to different types of life; cultured with the arts, fashion, and books as the central core. <br><br>She thrived and continued to college... and experienced life away from the safety net of the school she loved or her gran... thinking she deserved a little happiness now... only to have ugliness thrown back into her face again. <br><br>It was the final lesson which sealed the deal on her happiness/love lessons... it was not for her... best case scenario, she might get to be content.<br><br>Now what does all of this have to do with the communication style of Josie... well my sense is she may have been sophisticated with all of the world travel, fashion hobnobbing, and celebrity... but as to real life and interpersonal relationships .... she really only had her Gran... who was proper, from another era and was the only real influence she trusted... which made her in many ways extremely bright, able to accomplish much ...which she did... but very naive, too... almost like she came from another planet on some things.<br><br>And this is the biggest key which I felt the most.... she had created a facade... a false persona of a calm, collected, sure of herself confidant woman who she presented 24/7 for all to know... but the real girl, the one which her Gran knew was still hiding all these years was deep down still there...needing to come out... <br><br>Which brings me to Jake. Jake had his own facade... but it wasn't as clearly presented... he was this guy's guy; an accomplished professional fighter who had tasted fame and success. A man who also happened to have the capacity to love and love deeply. He had chosen poorly but still through all the hurt he had experienced... and it was deep... he had somehow left his heart open to love...but because of life... he wasn't clear he deserved it either. He not only was cut from the KA male template but he was a father too... and his love for all of his children was palpable through all of his actions. These kids were fully formed... and some of the best scenes in the book had to do with them.<br><br>But Gran knew... and she decided to intervene... <br><br>So here you have two people brought together through the love they had for the incredible force of Gran/Lydie... and by being respectful to her wishes... both Josie and Jake benefit.<br><br>There is too much to this love story for me to go into...KA structured this like all of her vintage KA books but without the side stories of explosions or fast-paced action. She held true to the vision she had about these two people and what it would be like for them to come together doing the KA mating dance. She did not disappoint at all. <br><br>She packed this book with so much sexual chemistry between these two, the combustion and power when they finally got together was epic.<br><br>I will briefly say the multiple characters in this book are all fantastic; humorous, smart, caring, and worthy of their own stories... whether combined with another or on their own... KA does not leave them out there floating around in our mind's eye wondering what is happening with them.<br><br>I will also say...as you all know, I can get a little long-winded about things I love... there are real, serious topics addressed in this book; teenage behavior, bullying, domestic abuse, parental abandonment, self-worth, and learning to believe in yourself and others. I could go into all types of details of how amazingly well done KA worked these topics into the story without us feeling overwhelmed.<br><br>Instead, I am just going to hope this review with my take on the main character, Josie might give those who couldn't connect another way to see her...or not. <br><br>Please read all of the terrific reviews out there... no matter the stars as.. I think all of them have something to say and take away...and then the best.....is you get to decide. <br><br>I must give a shout out to the <i> Amazing Buddy Read by The Canaries...</i> this was one of the most fun experiences I have had here on GR. This group of readers are accepting, passionate, hysterically funny, and downright terrific. Thank you so much... it was BEYOND :DDD<br><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20603820.The_Will__Magdalene___1_" title="The Will (Magdalene, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1390276224l/20603820._SY75_.jpg" alt="The Will (Magdalene, #1) by Kristen Ashley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <b>The Will (Magdalene, #1)<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/889941192">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24483320.Soaring__Magdalene___2_" title="Soaring (Magdalene, #2) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1421522757l/24483320._SY75_.jpg" alt="Soaring (Magdalene, #2) by Kristen Ashley" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> Soaring (Magdalene, #2)</b><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1230522733">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25165984.The_Time_in_Between__Magdalene___3_" title="The Time in Between (Magdalene, #3) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_808356489" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/808356489" />
    <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance"><img alt="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1376622739p2/5498948.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/808356489?book_show_action=true">Jan 01, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance">Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=auto-buy-authors">auto-buy-authors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=best-of-the-best">best-of-the-best</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=favorite-heroine">favorite-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=favorite-alpha-hero">favorite-alpha-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=faves">faves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=favorite-authors">favorite-authors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=keeper-shelf">keeper-shelf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=tissues-needed">tissues-needed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer808356489" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3900556865493264154"><b>5 KA has her magic back Stars</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396982363i/9213831._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png' width='50' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>It's never too late to reach for happiness and no matter what life has done to you, it's never too late to find it.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396467832ra/9138270.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>Oh yes!<br/>God yes!<br/>Fuck yes!</b><br/><br/>KA got her mojo back with this book. If I needed any further proof that the past releases lost the KA touch because of her publisher, this book was it. It was everything that I've been missing in her published books lately. And I do mean <b>every-fucking-thing</b>.<br/><br/>Who else but Kristen Ashley can take a heroine that talks like</span>
  <span id="freeText3900556865493264154" style="display:none"><b>5 KA has her magic back Stars</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396982363i/9213831._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">It's never too late to reach for happiness and no matter what life has done to you, it's never too late to find it.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396467832ra/9138270.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Oh yes!<br>God yes!<br>Fuck yes!</b><br><br>KA got her mojo back with this book. If I needed any further proof that the past releases lost the KA touch because of her publisher, this book was it. It was everything that I've been missing in her published books lately. And I do mean <b>every-fucking-thing</b>.<br><br>Who else but Kristen Ashley can take a heroine that talks like she's a Victorian maiden and not only make it so it doesn't irritate the living crap out of you, but actually endears her to you? No really? I ask you?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397069899ra/9226393.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Well, yes I can. Because it was fantastic!<br><br>Miss Ashley takes a prim and proper heroine that by all intents and purposes conducts herself like she has a stick up her ass the size of a palm tree and makes you love her. Josie was everything I love in a heroine and even some things that I'd normally hate...yet loved here. Here you have a heroine that shows up in a town and it's like the woman has a catnip pussy...uhem. All she has to do is breathe and she draws men to her like a bitch in heat.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397069899ra/9226394.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Normally, this would drive me batty. Here, I couldn't get enough. Such is the magic of KA.<br><br>Who else but KA can give you a hero that's equal parts sweet, slightly assholish, a dash domineering, a whole lot of jealous, with a twist of melt your panties dirty talker?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397069899ra/9226395.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Oh and make him a sexy as sin former boxer and an amazing single father in his late 40s?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381692395ra/5196098.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Who else but KA can give you a beautiful love story with the perfect burn of sexual tension all to explode in the most erotic way when they finally give into the inevitable?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394148173ra/8814143.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Don't believe me? Just wait till that halfway mark and see for yourself what I mean.<br><br>And finally, who else but KA can give you an ending and an epilogue that will leave you an ugly crying, sniveling, kindle hugging in the middle of your room mess?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397070773ra/9226564.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In case you're curious, those are rhetorical questions, because the answer to all those is NO ONE. Absolutely, positively NO ONE but Kristen Ashley.<br><br>I adored this book. I tried stretching it out as much as possible and yet couldn't find myself to put it down. I fell in love with Jake, I fell in love with his kids, I fell in love with the quirky Josie, and I completely and utterly fell in love with the story.<br><br>I won't give you a sum up of the book or what it's about since you can get the main gist of it from the book blurb. Giving you anything else will be an injustice to the KA reading experience. What I will tell you is that if you're anything like me and found her last few releases to be somewhat shy of lackluster, this will bring you out of that funk.<br><br>I know that I will only be sticking to her self-pubs from now on because she has definitely not lost her touch, it's simply been getting edited out by her publisher. And now I will be on pins and needles in pervy anticipation of Frankie and Benny's book.<br><br>Miss Ashley, I only have one thing to tell you after finishing this<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397070773ra/9226565.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>For more reviews visit<br><a href="http://dirtygirlromance.blogspot.com/" target="blogspot" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436206i/881587.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> </b></span>
  <a data-text-id="3900556865493264154" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1006309150" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1006309150" />
    <a title="Flo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7643503-flo"><img alt="Flo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597575025p2/7643503.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1006309150?book_show_action=true">Jul 25, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Flo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Flo" href="/user/show/7643503-flo">Flo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781311349538" href="/book/show/20332278-the-will">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=standalone">standalone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1006309150" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15414628723080015152"><b>5 **<u>lavender</u>** STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1455016674i/18041311.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Life is like a boxing match. Defeat is declared not when you fall but when you refuse to stand again.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>*sigh*<br/><br/>Wonderful. Epic. Just really very sweet and moving. A fabulous addition to my favourite Kristen Ashley reads. Yes, this is quite formulaic and I can assure you in the grand scheme of things, nothing I read here was really new in the KA universe. But who the hell cares. It's escapism at its best and as my partner in crime would say 'crack on paper'.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText15414628723080015152" style="display:none"><b>5 **<u>lavender</u>** STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1455016674i/18041311.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Life is like a boxing match. Defeat is declared not when you fall but when you refuse to stand again.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>*sigh*<br><br>Wonderful. Epic. Just really very sweet and moving. A fabulous addition to my favourite Kristen Ashley reads. Yes, this is quite formulaic and I can assure you in the grand scheme of things, nothing I read here was really new in the KA universe. But who the hell cares. It's escapism at its best and as my partner in crime would say 'crack on paper'.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“He’ll make you happy, my precious Josie.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>For twenty-three years <b>Josephine Malone</b> has lead a very fast and fascinating life, working as the PA for a very well known and successful Photographer. She is content with what she has got. There are things in her past that made her choose this kind of unpredictable and uncommitted life. The only thing constant and dear to her her heart was her grandmother - Lydia Malone, the woman who saved her, who gave her a home in the small town of Magdalene in Maine and the only person who ever really loved her. Naturally the day Josie found out her anker had died her whole life was changed - in more than one way.<br><br>As the title of the book suggests a will plays a bigger role in the story. Lydia Malone was a beautiful soul and she always wanted the best for her granddaughter. The best thing she had to share was <b>Jake Spears</b>. In her will she not only bequeaths Lavender House and all her belongings to her, she also gave Josie to Jake. Somewhat unconventional and amusing, if you ask me.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“It’s never too late to reach for happiness and no matter what life has done to you, it’s never too late to find it.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Jake is a father of three kids, an ex-boxer and the owner of both a boxing gym and a strip club. The best part, Josie never even knew he existed in her grandmother's life. The big question is why they had such a big connection Josie didn't know about and why Jake is so determined to honor Lydia's wishes. <br><br>A carefully executed seduction and persuasion plan ensues. Josie is not an easy nut to crack, but it sure is worth it for Jake and his kids.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I wanted you before I even knew you. Someone handsome and strong and protective and fierce. You’re everything I ever wanted, darling.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>A grandmother who pulls the strings from the grave, a charming and yet rough around the edges hero, a cute bunch of kids and a very classy and slightly odd heroine. That's the kind of old school KA I love and always fall for. The family dynamics, the humour and the very sexy couple make this an exceptional piece of escapism. A beautiful little world, in a small town where people care about each other and bad situations get resolved rather swiftly. It's just so gosh darn cute, I still feel like smiling when I think about it. <br><br>But don't let the cheese fool you, <i>The Will</i> made me actually cry. Especially towards the end I was sniffling like a crazy person. I love the emotional intimacy between the characters. It really got to me. And that's all you can hope for in a book, right?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.co.at/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1447539995i/17017465.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/coffeeaddictbooks?ref=tn_tnmn" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598100i/14852514.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://twitter.com/flo_reads" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852521.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852522.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/101016591301224002138" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852523.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/flocoffeeaddict/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431599699i/14852627.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_906851397" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/906851397" />
    <a title="Candace" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16384209-candace"><img alt="Candace" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459720769p2/16384209.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/906851397?book_show_action=true">Apr 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=sweet-heart-warming-stories">sweet-heart-warming-stories</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer906851397" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11922706022500163786">This was a really good book and while it didn't blow me away, it was highly enjoyable. I've been reading a lot of suspenseful, dark romance stories as of late. It was nice to change it up a bit with a nice, light and straightforward love story. Sometimes you just have to take a break from all those mysterious and emotionally traumatized romance-novel guys that always seem to lean towards bondage, etc. I love a bad boy, but it can be a bit overwhelming!<br/><br/>The characters and the storyline were very w</span>
  <span id="freeText11922706022500163786" style="display:none">This was a really good book and while it didn't blow me away, it was highly enjoyable. I've been reading a lot of suspenseful, dark romance stories as of late. It was nice to change it up a bit with a nice, light and straightforward love story. Sometimes you just have to take a break from all those mysterious and emotionally traumatized romance-novel guys that always seem to lean towards bondage, etc. I love a bad boy, but it can be a bit overwhelming!<br /><br />The characters and the storyline were very well-developed by Ms. Ashley, as is the norm for her. I also liked that the story of Josie and Jake seemed believable and not overdone in some fantastical way. The downside, is that sometimes the book did drag on. I did get bored a few times reading the detailed descriptions of mundane chores, etc. I think some of those details could have been skipped without taking anything from the story.<br /><br />Despite a few lulls, I did enjoy this story a great deal and I do recommend it.<br /><br />Check out more of my reviews at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.bookaddicthaven.com">www.bookaddicthaven.com</a> </span>
  <a data-text-id="11922706022500163786" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <b>I loved it Fuckuva Lot!</b>

The writing was exquisite, the story captivating, the characters wonderful.<br><br>Josie is hands down the best heroine ever. She was so classy, wise and with a heart of gold. I adore Josie. I envy Josie. I wanna be Josie. This woman is pure perfection, not a thing I would change. <br><br>And Jake was as perfect as Josie was. <b>
  <i>"She thinks I'm the shit."</i>
</b> Oh yes Jake, yes you are. He was rough on the outside with his foul language and boxing as a hobby, but so gooey, sweet, warm and tender on the inside. Good father, good friend, good man. <br><br>It was a beautiful, drama free story about second chances in life, about falling in love and finding happiness again, about finally having the family the main characters always dreamt of. Also, about the fact that being content is sometimes not enough in life, that you need to be happy and it's never too late to look for that happiness. <br><br>This book was pure perfection, nothing else to add. Now, if her other books are as good as this one, I'm gonna eat that shit up!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431871206ra/14877428.gif" width="400”/&gt;&lt;br /&gt;" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
