  <span id="freeText13127484607019608995" style="display:none"> <b>"Don't know,Josie."<br> "Just know whatever it is I want you to be<br> a part of it and I hope like fuck you want<br> the same." </b><br><br>+6 STARS &lt;333<br><br>Wow AMAZING like the most books of Kristen Ashley...This woman whatever she wrote is fantastic!!!I was hooked from the beginning until the end!Such a beautiful,hot,emotional,sexy and completely sensual book!I really liked Josie and Jake and I was sucked in to their story!I am hopeful that this will be another great series by Kristen Ashley!!!<br><br>Josie is a 45 years old who has been traveling around the world as an assistant to a famous photographer.The last years she didn't have a serious relationship.The only people she loved so much now has passed away and she must go back for the funeral..This person was her grandmother..who was there for her when her father abused her...She is surprised when a man she doesn't know is the other person at the reading of the will.<br> Her grandmother gives Josie the family home and quite a bit of money. She gives some money to Jake for his kid's.Josie is surprised because her grandmother never told Josie about Jake and his family. ..<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397516904i/9286464._SY540_.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><br>Jake and Josie start as friends..but soon they will become more...Jake and Josie’s relationship develops slowly and it was so sweet..<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397516755i/9286443.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>At the beginning I thought I will have problem because I'm 25 years old and I don't like to read about older people but this book was so beautiful that I didn't have problem with the ages!!Because the story was fantastic.. about two people finding love after life has given then only bad moments..<br><br>Josie was ok for me..I like how she was with Jake and his kids, my only complaint is about the way she was talking!Sometimes I need to re-read again what she said!Jake &lt;3 I'm in love!He is the reason I give this book 6 STARS !!He is an ex-boxer who live with his kids!I loved his dirty mouth!!!He is such an alpha male!!Exactly what I need it!!Sexy,hot and .I also fell in love with his kids who where amazing!!He cares for them and he wants the best!!Absolutely he is one of the best male characters Kristen have wrote!!<br><br><b>"He was the most beautiful thing I'd ever seen in my life."</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397516755ra/9286444.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And the epilogue &lt;3 *sigh* so beautiful!!Ican't wait for the next book!!<br><br> <a href="http://readmore-sleepless.blogspot.gr/" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_802646250" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/802646250" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/802646250?book_show_action=true">Dec 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781311349538" href="/book/show/20332278-the-will">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=dual-pov">dual-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=hot-hot-hot">hot-hot-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=2014-release">2014-release</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer802646250" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17878350429067894677"><br/>★★★★★ <b>5+ stars!</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“It’s never too late to reach for happiness and no matter what life has done to you, it’s never too late to find it.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397242423i/9253027.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Reading this book = being in <b>KA Heaven!!! <br/><br/>And it made me soooo happy.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380390852ra/752831.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Really, it did.<br/><br/>I was torn between devouring it like crazy or savoring every chapter of it, but in the end the devouring part won and I ended up reading it in 2 days. <b>The Will</b> has everything the perfect, standard KA story should have: a strong but quirky heroine, a fierce and protective </span>
  <span id="freeText17878350429067894677" style="display:none"><br>★★★★★ <b>5+ stars!</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“It’s never too late to reach for happiness and no matter what life has done to you, it’s never too late to find it.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397242423i/9253027.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Reading this book = being in <b>KA Heaven!!! <br><br>And it made me soooo happy.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380390852ra/752831.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Really, it did.<br><br>I was torn between devouring it like crazy or savoring every chapter of it, but in the end the devouring part won and I ended up reading it in 2 days. <b>The Will</b> has everything the perfect, standard KA story should have: a strong but quirky heroine, a fierce and protective alpha male, a huge amount of loopy and unique side characters, an interesting and captivating plot, some drama, lots of sexual tension and a fantastic epilogue. ♥<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397337614i/9264921.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Josephine Malone</b> is a 45 year old assistant to the famous fashion photographer Henry Gagnon and she's perfectly content with her life the way it is. Travelling all over the world, meeting famous artists and supermodels, wearing the latest couture and fashion outfits, eating in the finest restaurants. Her life has all the luxury she could want. Events from her past however have made her pull up a disguise for the past 23 years that makes her come off as cold and aloof. To protect her own heart, she's built up a barrier and refuses to let anyone in. Relationships aren't her thing and she's decided she's perfectly fine with casuals flings. The only person truly close to her is her grandmother, Lydie Malone. And maybe her boss, Henry, whom she's been in (unrequited) love with for the past 23 years.<br><br>Now, she's lost one of those two people. Her grandmother Lydie has died and she has to return to the small town Magdalene in Maine to attend her funeral and hear her will being read. While she's there she stays in her grandmother's Lavender House, the one place she truly calls home and she meets the mysteriously handsome Jake Spear...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397337614i/9264922.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Jake Spear</b> is an ex-boxer, strip club owner and father of three children. He's been married three times and each and every time those marriages have been a failure. Despite his bad choices in love, he's a respectable and upstanding citizen of the small town of Magdalene, a caring father to his children and he's been a close friend to Lydie for the past 7 years. Throughout these years Lydie has told him much about her granddaughter Josie and everything she's told has been good. So good even that, combined with the pictures she's shown him of her, he's come to care about her as well even though he's never met her in person.<br><br>When they meet shortly after Lydie's funeral, Josie has no idea who he is since her grandmother has never talked about him throughout the years she's known him and his family. But when Lydie's Will is read, Jake and Josie both find out how much Lydie thought the two of them would be a perfect match to each other.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"My most precious possession, the thing I treasure about anything else in this world, that being my granddaughter, Josephine Diana Malone, I hereby bequeath to James Markham Spear.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Even though Josie finds it bizarre that her grandmother would "bequeath" her to a man she's never met, she and Jake start to hang out and get to know each other as friends. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"What's next?" I queried. <br><br>"Don't know, Josie. Just know whatever it is I want you to be a part of it and I hope like fuck you want the same."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Jake and Josie's love is like a slow burning candle. Even though they both have feelings for each other from the start, they both have their own reasons for taking things slow and letting the foundation of their relationship grow strong before taking the next step. With her being so proper and well spoken (which at first annoyed me but started to grow on me throughout the story) and him being so no-nonsense and rough, they couldn't have been more different but somehow they made perfect sense together and they complemented each other perfectly! <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I never wanted anything but you, Jake… And I wanted you before I even knew you… You’re everything I ever wanted, darling.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Of course, there are some obstacles to overcome before they find their happiness. There's some drama and a bit of angst, but not a huge amount of it. And even though this book is a long one, I enjoyed every single page of it and when it was over all I could think was that I want <i>more</i>. Josie and Jake's story had me hooked from an it might even be one of my new favorite KA stories EVER. All in all, this was the PERFECT start to a new series and I'm already anxiously awaiting the next tale in the Magdalene series. :)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397337614i/9264923.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="17878350429067894677" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=2014">2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer802601632" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1663184209818975699"><b>6 KA, Vintage, Dreamy Stars<br/><br/><i>Follow your heart</i></b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398277118i/9394608._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>A house in lavender.<br/><br/>A woman that forgot to live.<br/><br/>A man with the courage to try his hand.<br/><br/>And the will of an old lady, that will bind them forever.</i><br/><br/><b>♪♫ I need a hero<br/>I'm holding out for a hero 'til the end of the night<br/>He's gotta be strong<br/>And he's gotta be fast<br/>And he's gotta be fresh from the fight<br/>I need a hero<br/>I'm holding out for a hero 'til the morning light<br/>He's gotta be sure<br/>And it's gotta be soon<br/>And he's gotta be larger than life ♪♫</b><br/><br/>It's never to late to rea</span>
  <span id="freeText1663184209818975699" style="display:none"><b>6 KA, Vintage, Dreamy Stars<br><br><i>Follow your heart</i></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398277118i/9394608._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>A house in lavender.<br><br>A woman that forgot to live.<br><br>A man with the courage to try his hand.<br><br>And the will of an old lady, that will bind them forever.</i><br><br><b>♪♫ I need a hero<br>I'm holding out for a hero 'til the end of the night<br>He's gotta be strong<br>And he's gotta be fast<br>And he's gotta be fresh from the fight<br>I need a hero<br>I'm holding out for a hero 'til the morning light<br>He's gotta be sure<br>And it's gotta be soon<br>And he's gotta be larger than life ♪♫</b><br><br>It's never to late to reach for love, to earn the happiness that life owes you. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398277118i/9394609.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I admire KA for her ability to create worlds. Not fantastic ones, though I adore them as well and I want to live in them. What I mean, is her ability to recreate a real world that we all dream about. She takes all our hopes and smiles, fantasies and memories and she builds entire lives. Lives, that each one of us would be glad to live in. She doesn’t exaggerate. Her characters are me, you, my best friend and my gran. People that you can relate to, talk to, laugh and cry with them. Perfect you said? No, certainly. They curse, they stumble, fall, make stupid choices and mistakes. That’s why they are fun to read about. Because at the end you realize that you read a story about you. And the Christian Louboutin shoes you always dreamt about having…. ;)<br><br>So I could say that this is Jake and Josephine’s story. A story about two people in their forties who have lived but not loved until they found each other. I could go on and tell you about Jake being a boxer and Josephine having an amazing taste in clothes and talking in elaborate words. I could start gossiping about Jake’s kids, their relationships, Alyssa, omelets in The Shack, the gym, the strip joint and photographers too proud and blind to admit to love. I could describe all these and gash about how much I loved it. I could also say that I understand some fellow reviewer's frustration about the inner-dialogues, the second-guessing, how the heroes somehow behaved like they were in their twenties instead of forties, but it's KA and I don't mind. <br><br>But I won’t. This is Jake and Josephine’s life and you deserve to read it on on your own, finish it with a sigh and left alone to daydream about what you need to do to fulfill your heart’s desire.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398277118i/9394610.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>Waiting for the book...</i><br><b>New KA Series!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380436734ra/882847.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380298628ra/686188.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Can't wait...</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="1663184209818975699" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_906320272" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/906320272" />
    <a title="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10336538-jessica-silverbow"><img alt="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1393785730p2/10336538.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/906320272?book_show_action=true">Apr 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " href="/user/show/10336538-jessica-silverbow">Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=the-heart-wants-what-the">the-heart-wants-what-the</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=meh">meh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=indie">indie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer906320272" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2254393715699508896">I love Kristen Ashley. I do. I don't even care, you naysayers can naysay all you want, and I'll still love her.<br/><br/>But that's turning more and more into a cumulative thing . . .<br/><br/>B/c I have no idea what is going on here. This was like KA as seen through opaque glass: you can make out the staple features if you squint really hard, but mostly it's a big ol' blurry mess that only vaguely resembles the standard KA that sits out in the open. And I've come to expect that from anything we get from KA via a p</span>
  <span id="freeText2254393715699508896" style="display:none">I love Kristen Ashley. I do. I don't even care, you naysayers can naysay all you want, and I'll still love her.<br><br>But that's turning more and more into a cumulative thing . . .<br><br>B/c I have no idea what is going on here. This was like KA as seen through opaque glass: you can make out the staple features if you squint really hard, but mostly it's a big ol' blurry mess that only vaguely resembles the standard KA that sits out in the open. And I've come to expect that from anything we get from KA via a publisher (CHAOS series, the last couple of COLORADO MOUNTAIN installments . . .), but when BROKEN DOVE came out at Christmas time, AND ROCK CHICK REVOLUTION even before that, I breathed easier believing that independently published KA was still classic KA.<br><br>It would seem I breathed too soon. <br><br>So what was wrong with it?<br><br>1. Josie, Josie, Josie. I understand what KA was trying to do here, I really do, but she wayyyy over-shot. She was trying to create a false kind of hoity toity, high society type, a character who hides behind proper speech and big words. (Kind of like chicky-poo from FAIRYTALE COME ALIVE hid behind pretty clothes and decorous behavior.)<br><br>The problem with this is that readers will always have the largest vocabularies, b/c we read, it's what we do. And this:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397176704i/9242872.jpg" width="236" height="177" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>is a real problem. A problem from which one can infer that we know what people talk like in real life. <br><br>And Josie does <i>not</i> speak like a real, live person. Not a real, live person in the year of our Lord, 2014 anyway. She refers to Jake as a "pugilist." No really. She does. And, though I have absolutely no idea how, I actually knew what a pugilist was (it's a boxer). But one of my favorite things about reading on a kindle is having the OED at my fingertips. For anyone who doesn't know, that means that not only can I <i>define</i> words as I'm reading, I can also trace the word origin, which means I know that the word "pugilist" hasn't been used colloquially since the mid-18th century. She also insists on referring to Jake's children's friends as "young, insert-name-here." This happens most often with "boy Taylor"&lt;-----see, classic KA right-friggin'-there: Jake's daughter has two BFFs, girl Taylor and boy Taylor. <br><br>It's cute and quirky. Wanna know what's NOT cute and quirky? <br><br>"Alas, young Taylor . . . "<br><br>Over and over again. Not cute and quirky. Ridiculous. I had alternating images of Pierce (who lived 100(ish) years ago) from THE HOLLOWS "opining" this or that and an old Calvin &amp; Hobbes comic:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397178024i/9243059._SX540_.gif" width="600" height="189" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>2. Lack of villainous villains. (Non-paranormal) KA books are mostly romantic suspense. There's always a Bad Guy. A Bad Guy who's bad enough to need to be either killed, or imprisoned. <br><br>Not this time. <br><br>Oh sure, one dude is pretty smarmy, but mostly they're minor annoyances that don't even need Man-in-Uniform intervention&lt;-----LAME. And by "lame" I mean BORING.<br><br>3. Overall the plot was just MEH. Maybe it's b/c this is straight-up contemporary romance instead of romantic suspense, but nothing really interesting happens in the book. Tough Guy <i>was</i> keeping a Secret from Josie, but the Secret was pretty guessable, and it was one of those Secrets that's not much more than an insight into Tough Guy's psyche, meant to endear him to you. <br><br>*rolls eyes*<br><br>And the characters and relationships read like a mash-up of previous KA novels (mostly from <i>The 'Burg</i>). <br><br>So, yeah. Blah.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2254393715699508896" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText6987607719857808417" style="display:none"> <b>5 Lavender Stars.</b>	<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397059143i/9225111.jpg" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The only person Josie could trust and love unconditionally after being hurt in the past, just died. <div id="review_1617393465" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="⊱✿⊰ Alicia ⊱✿⊰ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34454544-alicia"><img alt="⊱✿⊰ Alicia ⊱✿⊰ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1480986441p2/34454544.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1617393465?book_show_action=true">Mar 08, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="⊱✿⊰ Alicia ⊱✿⊰ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="⊱✿⊰ Alicia ⊱✿⊰ " href="/user/show/34454544-alicia">⊱✿⊰ Alicia ⊱✿⊰ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34454544-alicia?shelf=2019-audio">2019-audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34454544-alicia?shelf=1st-in-series">1st-in-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34454544-alicia?shelf=fav-author">fav-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34454544-alicia?shelf=kristen-ashley">kristen-ashley</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1617393465" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5572521248640453719"><b>5 'Sally Forth' Stars</b><br/><br/>I listened to the audio, this had both positives and negatives.<br/><br/>Positive: This was a long book and I'm pretty sure I would have got a little bored if I'd read it.<br/><br/>Negative: The narrator seemed too old and snooty for the heroine and it took a while to get used to.<br/><br/>I get Josephine is 45 and posh but this narrator reminded me more of a 65 year old. In saying that by the end of the book I thought she'd done a brilliant job.<br/><br/><a href='https://s989.photobucket.com/user/Alicia_Mackey/media/Itssobeautiful_zpszwedqkqp.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1552047020ra/27172920.gif' alt=' photo Itssobeautiful_zpszwedqkqp.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>This was a beautiful love story with a unique story lin</span>
  <span id="freeText5572521248640453719" style="display:none"><b>5 'Sally Forth' Stars</b><br><br>I listened to the audio, this had both positives and negatives.<br><br>Positive: This was a long book and I'm pretty sure I would have got a little bored if I'd read it.<br><br>Negative: The narrator seemed too old and snooty for the heroine and it took a while to get used to.<br><br>I get Josephine is 45 and posh but this narrator reminded me more of a 65 year old. In saying that by the end of the book I thought she'd done a brilliant job.<br><br><a href="https://s989.photobucket.com/user/Alicia_Mackey/media/Itssobeautiful_zpszwedqkqp.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1552047020ra/27172920.gif" alt=" photo Itssobeautiful_zpszwedqkqp.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This was a beautiful love story with a unique story line that really caught my attention.<br><br><a href="http://s989.photobucket.com/user/Alicia_Mackey/media/Josephine_zpsqlwvohln.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1552047020i/27172921.jpg" alt=" photo Josephine_zpsqlwvohln.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>As I said above it took me some time to warm to Josephine, as at first I thought she was an uppity bitch who looked down her nose at everyone thank god I was wrong! Really Josephine was hiding behind this facade making sure no one could get too close. When you learn about her childhood you can see why she is the way she is.<br><br><a href="http://s989.photobucket.com/user/Alicia_Mackey/media/Jake_zpsrzsol5hh.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1552047020ra/27172922.gif" alt=" photo Jake_zpsrzsol5hh.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Jake is AWESOME!! He is a single dad of three kids, all of which are fantastic and I loved how Josephine made a personal connection with each child. Jake had been married three times and at first he came across as a bit of a ladies man/man whore but really he just fell for the wrong women. He owns a strip club and boxing gym and works really hard to keep them afloat to support his kids.<br><br>Jake boxes and I think I'd be like the other ladies and love 'fight night'.<br><br>When Jake and Josephine come together the chemistry is off the charts!!<br><br><a href="https://s989.photobucket.com/user/Alicia_Mackey/media/sexyscene_zps9np7ynoe.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1552047020ra/27172923.gif" alt=" photo sexyscene_zps9np7ynoe.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I can honestly say I have never loved a character in a book that had died before the book had even started, but I fell hard for Gran in this one. It started with the reading of the Will and she shattered me at the end with her recorded message that had me needing a lot of tissues.<br><br>Jake and Josephine were just meant to be! They have an amazing story that everyone should read. A true timeless romance, I loved it!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="5572521248640453719" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=april-2014">april-2014</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer904311524" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5752111734760919156">**3.75 Lavender stars**<br/><br/>When I saw the cover of this book I felt it was calling my name to read it. It's so pretty!!! Yes, I judged a book by its cover. <blockquote>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396930357i/9205753._SY540_.jpg' width='150' height='220' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</blockquote>The death of <b>Josephine's</b> grandmother, Lydie, has brought her back to the Lavender House. The only house that Josephine has ever felt like it was home to her. <br/><br/>At the reading of the will she learns that her grandmother has left her to a man. This unconventional request starts the ball rolling in the love story between a prim and proper, <i>Mary Po</i></span>
  <span id="freeText5752111734760919156" style="display:none">**3.75 Lavender stars**<br><br>When I saw the cover of this book I felt it was calling my name to read it. It's so pretty!!! Yes, I judged a book by its cover. <blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396930357i/9205753._SY540_.jpg" width="150" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote>The death of <b>Josephine's</b> grandmother, Lydie, has brought her back to the Lavender House. The only house that Josephine has ever felt like it was home to her. <br><br>At the reading of the will she learns that her grandmother has left her to a man. This unconventional request starts the ball rolling in the love story between a prim and proper, <i>Mary Poppins type</i>, <b>Josephine</b>, and a rough around the edges, <b>Jake</b>. <br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>My man is going to be strong and tall and handsome and smart and protective and fierce, so very FIERCE, and wonderful and he's going to adore me.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><b>Josephine </b>has the same problem that Gwen from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12299419.Mystery_Man__Dream_Man___1_" title="Mystery Man (Dream Man, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Mystery Man</a> encountered; a bunch of hot eligible guys wanting to date her. I'm going to predict that the next two books in this series will feature - Amond and Mickey. And like her <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16163690.Own_the_Wind__Chaos___1_" title="Own the Wind (Chaos, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Own the Wind</a> series she might do a spin off with Jake's kids. <br><br> <b>Jake</b> is a parent of teenagers and so am I (three highschoolers). Teens can be handful at times and at this stage of child development we as parents are faced with a whole new set of worries: driving, dating, (teen) drama, etc. Sometimes just listening to my three teenagers I feel like I'm living in a <i>young adult</i> book. I like the dynamics Jake's children brought to the overall story. <br><br><b>SERIES:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20332278.The_Will__Magdalene_Series___1_" title="The Will (Magdalene Series, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1389968679s/20332278.jpg" alt="The Will (Magdalene Series, #1) by Kristen Ashley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>The Magdalene Series is a new series starting in 2014. It will be a trilogy of romances set in the fictional town of Magdalene, Maine. To find out when the next two books will be released <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/119018-magdalene-series" rel="nofollow noopener">click here.</a></span>

<div id="review_827558748" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/827558748" />
    <a title="Ingie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15589375-ingie"><img alt="Ingie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1477339772p2/15589375.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/827558748?book_show_action=true">Jan 18, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ingie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ingie" href="/user/show/15589375-ingie">Ingie</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/24809101-the-will">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=books-i-read-2015">books-i-read-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=romance-m-f-audio">romance-m-f-audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=romance-m-f-contemporary">romance-m-f-contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=series-standalone-stories">series-standalone-stories</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer827558748" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9232198957475270708"><i>Written May 20, 2015.</i><br/><br/><b>4 1/2 Stars - Adorable, adorable and so touching sweet</b><br/><blockquote>
<a href='http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Diverse/5a278a52-6c68-4f8d-bd0e-bfebc33ca70e_zpsc0vknixz.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422994522i/13573686.jpg' alt=' photo 5a278a52-6c68-4f8d-bd0e-bfebc33ca70e_zpsc0vknixz.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/>‘It would be much easier if he was less wonderful.’</blockquote><br/>Can you rightly call a book <u>adorable</u>? If it's possible this one is just that. An adorable, charming, heartwarming romance novel. A story about everything and nothing. A very long book (and even longer audiobook - freaking 23:30 hrs - imagine, it's a lot of time!!). <br/><br/>It's always with some angst I start a new book by <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley' title='Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kristen Ashley</a> — Will it be a winner or not?. I got this </span>
  <span id="freeText9232198957475270708" style="display:none"><i>Written May 20, 2015.</i><br><br><b>4 1/2 Stars - Adorable, adorable and so touching sweet</b><br><blockquote>
<a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Diverse/5a278a52-6c68-4f8d-bd0e-bfebc33ca70e_zpsc0vknixz.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422994522i/13573686.jpg" alt=" photo 5a278a52-6c68-4f8d-bd0e-bfebc33ca70e_zpsc0vknixz.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br>‘It would be much easier if he was less wonderful.’</blockquote><br>Can you rightly call a book <u>adorable</u>? If it's possible this one is just that. An adorable, charming, heartwarming romance novel. A story about everything and nothing. A very long book (and even longer audiobook - freaking 23:30 hrs - imagine, it's a lot of time!!). <br><br>It's always with some angst I start a new book by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley" title="Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley</a> — Will it be a winner or not?. I got this one (as an audiobook incl the kindle ebook) for just over $3 and was quite sure that it should turn out to be a bargain. So it was....of course. <br><br>*********************************************************<br><br><b>I liked, loved and enjoyed <i>The Will</i></b> from the first to the last page. Simply ADORABLE! ~ Terrific and wonderful well narrated by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/8304250.Hollis_McCarthy" title="Hollis McCarthy" rel="nofollow noopener">Hollis McCarthy</a>. <br><blockquote>
<a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Wear/shoes/ee61ae6e-6bb8-4622-872c-d339352792bc_zpsigoqmj7i.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431804271i/14869355.jpg" alt=" photo ee61ae6e-6bb8-4622-872c-d339352792bc_zpsigoqmj7i.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>‘Handbags and shoes were my passion.’<br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Diverse/5a278a52-6c68-4f8d-bd0e-bfebc33ca70e_zpsc0vknixz.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422994522i/13573686.jpg" alt=" photo 5a278a52-6c68-4f8d-bd0e-bfebc33ca70e_zpsc0vknixz.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a>
</blockquote><br><b><i>The Will</i> is a story about a strange gift in a will.</b><br><br><b>Josephine Malone</b>, a 45 years old woman trotting the globe as an assistant to a famous fashion photographer. When her very beloved grandma <i>Lydia</i> pass away Josie is back in her grandma's beautiful old big <i>Magdalene, Main</i> house. <br><br>Already at the funeral is Josie watching a stunning goodlooking man. It is a, since long, retired boxer <b>Jake Spear</b> (47 and still attractive and über sexy). He is there with his three children (two teens and a younger boy) and later it turns out that Josie's grandmother felt very much for this man and his three children.<br><br>Grandma Lydia's will has a quite remarkable gift, or perhaps a kind of future hope for a woman and a man which yet has to find the "perfect right one". She had a wish about a perfect match. <br><blockquote>
<a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Diverse/5a278a52-6c68-4f8d-bd0e-bfebc33ca70e_zpsc0vknixz.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422994522i/13573686.jpg" alt=" photo 5a278a52-6c68-4f8d-bd0e-bfebc33ca70e_zpsc0vknixz.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br>“It’s never too late to reach for happiness and no matter what life has done to you, it’s never too late to find it.”<br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/City%20and%20nature%20etc/Flowers/image.jpg14_zpsuy2x0ocm.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431697437i/14860675.jpg" alt=" photo image.jpg14_zpsuy2x0ocm.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a>
</blockquote><br>I longed for that first kiss, and I had to wait, but when it come, and more with that, it was greeeaaat. Gosh, Ms Ashley for sure know how to "wake up" a slumbering lady. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ @45% in the boxing arena: Hot, hard and sooo d@mn sweet. Mmmm!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Then we got a bumpy ride —heartbreaking and heartwarming— to a nice grand (family) HEA end and a adorable sweet KA epilogue. ~ Awww, awesome as always. <br><br>*********************************************************<br><br><b>This had been a five stars review</b> if at least 100 pages (or 5 hours) had been stripped away. Ms. Ashley is awesome, but sometimes she gets tedious. Finally are there pretty much text and story about nothing, and my patience is long but not infinite. <br><blockquote>“Stick with me,” he urged. <br>My voice was still trembling when I agreed, “All right.” <br>“All right, baby,” he said gently before he dipped his head and touched his mouth to mine. <br>And this time, having had him, having given him me, that touch was even sweeter.’<br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Diverse/5a278a52-6c68-4f8d-bd0e-bfebc33ca70e_zpsc0vknixz.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422994522i/13573686.jpg" alt=" photo 5a278a52-6c68-4f8d-bd0e-bfebc33ca70e_zpsc0vknixz.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a>
</blockquote><br>Enough.... I've spent so much time with these (adorable) characters and it's time to move on. You all knew I loved it by now. ~ Sincerely recommended as an audiobook listening (if you have a lot of free time) too. <br><br><b>I LIKE - sweet tales with mature grownups, interesting families and funny friends</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/826523239" />
    <a title="♥Sharon♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12125670-sharon"><img alt="♥Sharon♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417537732p2/12125670.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/826523239?book_show_action=true">Jan 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥Sharon♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥Sharon♥" href="/user/show/12125670-sharon">♥Sharon♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781311349538" href="/book/show/20332278-the-will">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer826523239" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6245909796707847689">5 Lovely Stars<br/><br/><a href='http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/thewill_zpse0b50e10.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397059720i/9225162.jpg' alt=' photo thewill_zpse0b50e10.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>In true Kristen Ashley fashion she gave us such a beautiful story of family, friends and love. This is my 28th book by KA and at the top of my absolute favorites list is Sweet Dreams, At Peace and Motorcycle Man. I have to say The Will is going to be added to that list. ❤<br/><br/>I really was in heaven while reading The Will. That might sound a bit corny but it’s true. It was like someone took hold of my hand and patiently guided me through the story of Josephine (Josie) Malone and Jake</span>
  <span id="freeText6245909796707847689" style="display:none">5 Lovely Stars<br><br><a href="http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/thewill_zpse0b50e10.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397059720i/9225162.jpg" alt=" photo thewill_zpse0b50e10.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>In true Kristen Ashley fashion she gave us such a beautiful story of family, friends and love. This is my 28th book by KA and at the top of my absolute favorites list is Sweet Dreams, At Peace and Motorcycle Man. I have to say The Will is going to be added to that list. ❤<br><br>I really was in heaven while reading The Will. That might sound a bit corny but it’s true. It was like someone took hold of my hand and patiently guided me through the story of Josephine (Josie) Malone and Jake Spear.<br> <br>I’m not going to say much about the plot because I think to fully enjoy their story you should go in with no more than what you read in the synopsis. To be truthful though, I read bits and pieces of some reviews just to appease my curiosity about a couple of things but that was about it.<br> <br>One of the things I loved about this story was that both Josie and Jake were in their 40’s and had live life a bit. Josie was stunningly beautiful, spoke very graciously, and had a kind soul. Things that happened to Josie in the past has snuffed out her inner light. She led a good life though. She worked in high fashion, jetted off to beautiful countries and had all that material things she could want. But she truly wasn’t living the life she should be. Jake was warmhearted, caring and compassionate. He owned a boxing gym and a strip club that had him spread very thin but he didn’t care. He lived his life loving and providing for his three children. But when it came to matters of the heart Jake fell a bit short.<br><br><a href="http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/TheWill_zps2be0fe47.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397232588i/9251326.jpg" alt=" photo TheWill_zps2be0fe47.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This just wasn’t Josie and Jake’s story it was very much Conner, Amber and Ethan’s story too. Conner is strong and handsome like his dad, Amber is beautiful inside and out but just didn’t realize it all the time and Ethan he was a darling (he was my favorite). They were all navigating through the things that were being thrown their way. Each of them growing and learning about life’s little and sometimes painful lessons. Josie was so naturally loving and protective to Jake’s kids and I loved that about her. <br><br><a href="http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/thewill1_zpsb8db93c1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397232588i/9251327.jpg" alt=" photo thewill1_zpsb8db93c1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And I loved all the little things that happened in this book too. The funny moments at the dinner table or while watching TV, the forehead kisses Jake would give Josie, the girl conversations between Josie and Alyssa (a good friend) and Ethan thinking Jake and Josie kissing all the time was gross. <br> <br>So if you have read books by Kristen Ashley before I know you will love this one too. If you haven’t then start by reading The Will. If you enjoy books about family, friends and a good love story, then you will truly enjoy this one!❤<br><br>In closing, though we didn’t get a chance to know Gran, she was certainly was a wise women. :) <br><br>~ Gran wanted her to have a good life, a happy life, safe with people she cared about and trusted. And she got that by having Jake.<br><br><a href="http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/Thewill2_zps586d3ca1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397232589i/9251328.jpg" alt=" photo Thewill2_zps586d3ca1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="6245909796707847689" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_826308122" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/826308122" />
    <a title="Angela Bee Bee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8872735-angela-bee-bee"><img alt="Angela Bee Bee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1450418478p2/8872735.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/826308122?book_show_action=true">Jan 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angela Bee Bee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angela Bee Bee" href="/user/show/8872735-angela-bee-bee">Angela Bee Bee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 2940045582384" href="/book/show/21858319-the-will">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8872735-angela-bee-bee?shelf=want-to-re-read">want-to-re-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8872735-angela-bee-bee?shelf=everyone-loved-it-but-me">everyone-loved-it-but-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8872735-angela-bee-bee?shelf=preordered">preordered</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer826308122" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14793694118504769377">amazon--><a href='http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00HYIF9FW/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&camp=1789&creative=390957&creativeASIN=B00HYIF9FW&linkCode=as2&tag=angedi-20&linkId=UITP4J4G552MFKAC' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Will (The Magdalene Series Book 1)</a><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412026553i/11313036.gif' width='1' height='1' alt='' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Indeed (76 occurrences). <br/>Further (72).<br/>Thus (101).</i>
</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397486620ra/9281954.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>This woman does not snack. Ever. She doesn't enjoy sport. She doesn't like kids. She doesn't hug. She's never walked holding a man's hand. She's never had a home (she lived in her boss's pool house).<br/>She's a cold fish.<br/>It's a disguise, preventing people from getting close and hurting her.<br/>I think she's not meant to be likable and the intended appeal is the softening heart of the fashion diva, like Wi</span>
  <span id="freeText14793694118504769377" style="display:none">amazon--&gt;<a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00HYIF9FW/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=390957&amp;creativeASIN=B00HYIF9FW&amp;linkCode=as2&amp;tag=angedi-20&amp;linkId=UITP4J4G552MFKAC" rel="nofollow noopener">The Will (The Magdalene Series Book 1)</a><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412026553i/11313036.gif" width="1" height="1" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>Indeed (76 occurrences). <br>Further (72).<br>Thus (101).</i>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397486620ra/9281954.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This woman does not snack. Ever. She doesn't enjoy sport. She doesn't like kids. She doesn't hug. She's never walked holding a man's hand. She's never had a home (she lived in her boss's pool house).<br>She's a cold fish.<br>It's a disguise, preventing people from getting close and hurting her.<br>I think she's not meant to be likable and the intended appeal is the softening heart of the fashion diva, like Wilhemena in Ugly Betty or Meryl Streep in The Devil Wears Prada.<br>Her cluelessness and lack of life experience are meant to show her vulnerability. And your supposed to feel compassion for this fish out of water, lost, lonely girl.<br><br><i>Suffice it to say, </i>I just did not buy it. I did not feel the magic. Except with Amond. I want some Amond Joy dark chocolate yummy love.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397710605ra/9316267.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I liked Jake's pov, I liked the pillow talk and the sex.<br>But, I was turned off by Jake's three failed marriages, and the titty bar, regardless if it's "respectable".<br>I would have liked to see Josie helping them get real jobs instead of straightening their hair. Or even a modeling gig?<br><br>The intention here was that Jake is redeemed depite his shaky past, a sort of anti-hero theme. Similar to Knight, which I also didn't care for. <br>Jake is supposedly insecure of his worthiness of this chick, but his thoughts and actions are not consistent with that.<br><br>So both characters present this sort of ironic situation, that just didn't resonate with me. <br><b>A damaged Mary Poppins is rescued from her self imposed isolation by this insecure titty bar owner with a bad track record.</b><br>It's supposed to be polar opposites conquer all despite their circumstances, but the juxtaposition was too much here for me to believe it.<br><br>I also really disliked that the whole boxing arena knew about the locker room and cheered. <br>I didn't like her meddling in teen drama and her lying.<br>I didn't like the children being abandoned by their real mothers and substituting Josie.<br>I totally gave up when she kissed another guy, and Jake didn't go ballistic.<br><br>I may return to this when I'm in a less sour mood. But today ain't the day I'm gonna finish this behemoth.<br>I did change my mind on a second read of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12012999.Golden_Trail__The__Burg___3_" title="Golden Trail (The 'Burg, #3) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Golden Trail</a>, which was very similar to this.<br>I personally like the new concise streamlined KA style, and do not need all the details from this chick's brain.<br><br>I would not rec this to KA virgins. Start with The Gamble, but Not This.<br>I still absolutely adore and respect KA's mad genius, this one I just didn't buy in.<br><br> *****************<br><br>Before release; <b> People please dont rate til it comes out or you've read the arc.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389980322i/8118854._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And that is lavender on the cover. I thought it was lupine, but I was wrong. They have been photoshopped, but they are lavender. Lavandula angustifolia.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394323460i/8836586.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="14793694118504769377" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Ⓐlleskelle - teamSøren♗ ⊲I like big b00ks⊳" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18387313-lleskelle---teams-ren-i-like-big-b00ks"><img alt="Ⓐlleskelle - teamSøren♗ ⊲I like big b00ks⊳" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1599759753p2/18387313.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/802582625?book_show_action=true">Dec 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ⓐlleskelle - teamSøren♗ ⊲I like big b00ks⊳" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ⓐlleskelle - teamSøren♗ ⊲I like big b00ks⊳" href="/user/show/18387313-lleskelle---teams-ren-i-like-big-b00ks">Ⓐlleskelle - teamSøren♗ ⊲I like big b00ks⊳</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Everyone.</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18387313-lleskelle---teams-ren-i-like-big-b00ks?shelf=contemp">contemp</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18387313-lleskelle---teams-ren-i-like-big-b00ks?shelf=enemies-to-lovers">enemies-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18387313-lleskelle---teams-ren-i-like-big-b00ks?shelf=single-parent">single-parent</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18387313-lleskelle---teams-ren-i-like-big-b00ks?shelf=03-i-loved-like-a-lot">03-i-loved-like-a-lot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18387313-lleskelle---teams-ren-i-like-big-b00ks?shelf=hea">hea</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18387313-lleskelle---teams-ren-i-like-big-b00ks?shelf=00-on-my-ipad">00-on-my-ipad</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer802582625" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7189868715438280217">⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<b> 5 stars </b>⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br/><br/>I am sure I can’t make justice to the masterpiece I just read. I will simply try to tell you how it felt for me and what you can expect to find in it, leaving to you the privilege of meeting Josephine and Jake in The Will.<br/><blockquote>
  <b>“My most precious possession, the thing I treasure above anything else in this world … I hereby bequeath to …”</b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397165531i/9241033._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>There is a something to say about Kristen Ashley.<br/>She has her unique way to draw you in a world for you to wish it existed.<br/>She is one of</span>
  <span id="freeText7189868715438280217" style="display:none">⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<b> 5 stars </b>⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br><br>I am sure I can’t make justice to the masterpiece I just read. I will simply try to tell you how it felt for me and what you can expect to find in it, leaving to you the privilege of meeting Josephine and Jake in The Will.<br><blockquote>
  <b>“My most precious possession, the thing I treasure above anything else in this world … I hereby bequeath to …”</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397165531i/9241033._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>There is a something to say about Kristen Ashley.<br>She has her unique way to draw you in a world for you to wish it existed.<br>She is one of a few authors to tell tales about what I’d like to consider real people.<br><blockquote>
  <b>“…although it feels lovely you wish for me to have all kinds of beauty, I’m perfectly happy without it.”</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397163533i/9240672._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I remember perfectly well the first time I read a Kristen Ashley book, it was Mystery man. I couldn’t believe the jewel i had in my hands. I asked myself out loud "where have you been all this time?" I devoured it.<br>I think I read 5 KA’s book that week. I wanted to stay in her world and never coming back to reality.<br>This was only a year ago and by now I have read all her books. Some of them several times.<br><blockquote>
  <b> "I can't read all that in babe, Jake." - "You'll learn to read my babes."</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397163533i/9240673._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>See, every time I open KA’s books I lose myself in them. The characters talk to you. You forget you are reading a story, they are real. So real they push emotions your way that I can guarantee are very real. They make mistakes. They are certainly not perfect.<br>If you have ever read a Kristen Ashley’s book you know what I’m rambling about. <br><br>If this is your first time or chance to read one of her books, I hope you’ll fall in love just like I did with her descriptions, her "talk", her alpha males, feisty heroines and beautiful families. I hope you will feel as much as I do when I open her books. <br><blockquote>
  <b> "Every inch of you, outside and any way you can get inside, baby, physically or emotionally, is mine."</b>
</blockquote><br>The Magdalene series is a little different than her others series, there is no action or full drama, little by little and page after page you are taken along the road of Josie and Jake lives. You’ll get to know them, their family, their past, their yearnings. <br><blockquote>
  <b>"Don't know, Josie. Just know whatever it is I want you to be a part of it and I hope like fuck you want the same."</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397225627i/9250415._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>You will learn that life doesn’t end at forty. That your past does not define who you are. <br>That something you were missing all your life could still be found. That something you felt underserving of is in fact very <i>
  <b>righteous</b>
</i>.<br>It is really a slow paced journey, a peaceful one in Magdalene, Maine. So take your time reading it, enjoy your time there.<br><blockquote>
  <b>"Life is like a boxing match. Defeat is declared not when you fall but when you refuse to stand again."</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397163533i/9240674._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>One thing this author can write like no other is certainly her epilogues. She is the Queen. <br>A little advice in Kit’s books, when you see this little line "Epilogue", brace yourself. Because even if you were a sobbing mess already at the end of the story, this part of the book will make you fall. Hard.<br>You will feel it in the back of your throat, you will feel it prickling your eyes, you will try to contain it, but I can assure you the overwhelming twirl of emotions will make you cry happy tears like you never had for a book.<br><br><br><i><b>UPDATE APRIL 8, 2014</b><br>_______________________________________<br></i><br><b>THE WILL IS LIVE!!!<br>At least, it is in Europe. </b> <br>Go grab your copy <a> RIGHT HERE</a>!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396869764i/9196645._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396896388i/9200101._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396876493i/9197297._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396908456i/9202166._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="7189868715438280217" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1161165563" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously"><img alt="Rachel Reads Ravenously" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1539149211p2/14514998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1161165563?book_show_action=true">Jan 08, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel Reads Ravenously" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously">Rachel Reads Ravenously</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=new-adult-mania">new-adult-mania</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=kristen-ashley-aka-the-queen">kristen-ashley-aka-the-queen</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1161165563" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9771653732285576364"><b> 4 stars! </b><br/><br/><b> <i> " If you learn to accept yourself just as you are, learn to laugh at your quirks instead of hating them, show the world all that’s you without tryin’ to hide things that are not even a little unattractive, that makes you more attractive. What you got is a fuckuva lot. You own all of it and let it all hang out, you’ll go off-the-charts.” </i> </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/thewill.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420970307i/13301263.png' alt=' photo thewill.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>It's been a while since I've read a Kristen Ashley book. When I saw that pretty much all of my Goodreads friends were unanimous in loving this b</span>
  <span id="freeText9771653732285576364" style="display:none"><b> 4 stars! </b><br><br><b> <i> " If you learn to accept yourself just as you are, learn to laugh at your quirks instead of hating them, show the world all that’s you without tryin’ to hide things that are not even a little unattractive, that makes you more attractive. What you got is a fuckuva lot. You own all of it and let it all hang out, you’ll go off-the-charts.” </i> </b><br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/thewill.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420970307i/13301263.png" alt=" photo thewill.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It's been a while since I've read a Kristen Ashley book. When I saw that pretty much all of my Goodreads friends were unanimous in loving this book, I decided to jump back in with this one.<br><br>The story begins with Josie at the funeral of her beloved grandmother. Josie hasn't been back to Magdalene in years, as she was trotting the globe as an assistant to a famous photographer. Losing her Gran meant she had lost what was left of her family.<br><br>At the reading of her Gran's will, Josie discovers that her Gran has left Josie to Jake Spear. The former boxer and town strip club owner. At first Josie is horrified, by the idea and by Jake's profession, but over time and by getting to know him, Josie discovers there is more to Jake than meets the eye.<br><br><b> <i> “Life is like a boxing match. Defeat is declared not when you fall but when you refuse to stand again.” </i> </b><br><br>I was hesistant going into this book, as I'm in my mid-twenties and the main characters are in their forties. I was worried I wouldn't be interested in their romance or lives, but then I remembered how amazing Ashley's Sweet Dreams was, also about a couple in their forties, and decided to give this a chance. While this book does focus on issues that people in their forties face, like former lovers, ex wives, children and more, I still thoroughly enjoyed this book because it held strong themes of <b> family, love, survival, and finding one's place in life when things change abruptly. </b> <br><br>I loved the slow building romance between Josie and Jake, along with the little misunderstandings Josie had about Jake's interest. Josie's relationship with Jake's children was beautiful; she helped them without ever forcing her way in or being overbearing. She didn't try to be cool or someone different for their sakes, instead she was herself and showed constantly how much she cared about them and their well being. <br><br>The side plot with Henry made me kind of sad, I really hope he gets his own book or at least a mention of an HEA. I know he's the one who fucked things up with Josie, but come on. Men tend to not think things through all of the time. A lot of the time.<br><br><b> <i> “You see, a woman who knows herself and her worth knows that her time is valuable and her heart is precious. She doesn’t give either to a man who can’t respect the gifts he’s being offered.” </i> </b><br><br><b> ****MINI SPOILER AHEAD THAT I'M NOT TAGGING****</b><br>I only had two things I didn't really like about this book. One was the side plot about Conner and his five high school girlfriends. It didn't really make sense to me that Kristen Ashley would develop Ellie just to have them break up, with Conner being less than understanding of Ellie's position her parents put her in, just to find another different girlfriend by the end. I would rather have had Ellie not exist and use Sophie instead. It just seemed like a waste of plot to me, but I guess I'm just being nit-picky.<br><br>The other thing I REALLY did not like was the way Josie talked. It drove me up the wall! She sounded like a pretentious snob and everyone was like, "oh you talk weird, that's cute". I'm over here like, "um, no. She sounds incredibly rude and condescending" but whatever. Despite the way she talked, I still really liked Josie mostly because she had a heart of gold and when you were someone she cared about, she took care of you.<br><br>This book really did feel like one of Kristen Ashley's older works, and was a great romance that was well developed and not cheesy, which worked perfectly for me. That friggin epilogue had me crying giant ugly tears. Damn you KA! Right in the damn feels.<br><br><b> <i> “It’s never too late to reach for happiness and no matter what life has done to you, it’s never too late to find it.” </i> </b></span>
  <a data-text-id="9771653732285576364" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_856418537" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/856418537" />
    <a title="Spoiler Whore-Momoa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3531683-spoiler-whore-momoa"><img alt="Spoiler Whore-Momoa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1557708088p2/3531683.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/856418537?book_show_action=true">Feb 16, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Spoiler Whore-Momoa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Spoiler Whore-Momoa" href="/user/show/3531683-spoiler-whore-momoa">Spoiler Whore-Momoa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781311349538" href="/book/show/20332278-the-will">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer856418537" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11430166839663752341">First, I hate crying. Especially if it's over a book. Period. I get all red nosed, blotchy faced, red eyed demon looking. It's not pretty. Second. After I cry, I can't speak. My throat gets tight. It feels like there is a ball in my throat(get your mind outta the gutter) and I have to swallow hard(again, get your mind outta the gutter) repeatedly to talk and then when I do it goes something like this....I I I r r rre rreal rrreally lllloooove this booooook! WWWWWAAAAAA! It's beyond ridiculous. S</span>
  <span id="freeText11430166839663752341" style="display:none">First, I hate crying. Especially if it's over a book. Period. I get all red nosed, blotchy faced, red eyed demon looking. It's not pretty. Second. After I cry, I can't speak. My throat gets tight. It feels like there is a ball in my throat(get your mind outta the gutter) and I have to swallow hard(again, get your mind outta the gutter) repeatedly to talk and then when I do it goes something like this....I I I r r rre rreal rrreally lllloooove this booooook! WWWWWAAAAAA! It's beyond ridiculous. Seriously. Now, why did I mention that? Kit's epilogues are some of <b>THE</b> best out there. She is <b>LA REINA</b> of the epilogues. Third, it doesn't always mean that someone dies in a story. It can be a moment, a phrase or just how well a story is told that I just <b>GET</b> it. On to the story...<br /><br />Fate comes in many different shapes and forms. In this case in comes in The Will. In The Will, Josephine Malone's beloved grandmother left her in the hands to Jake Spears. They are both taken surprised to this. Josie and Jake are from two completely different worlds. You would think they wouldn't have anything in common but they do. <b>*</b><i>I'm gonna stop right here for a bit. When I read Josephine, I found her language on the nanny side being very proper. It kinda thru me off but I got over it and I'm pretty sure you will too. It teaches you to expand your vocabulary.</i><b>*</b> Now, with Kit's stories it's not all about the H and h. It's about family too and this family is one of the best I've read. The way Jake is with his kids is funny, adorable, laughable and men could learn a lesson or two. Of course there are side characters that are just as yummy and funny and you know that they'll get a story so I won't delve into them. In this story little by little, words by words, touch by touch it's revealed how even when someone is physically gone their presence is always felt with what special gift they left behind which is the power of love. Sometimes there are just no words that I can write down to do any justice to Kristen Ashley's books. I've been saying this for years but if you haven't read anything by her...<b>WHAT ARE YOU WAITING FOR!?!</b><br /><br /><b>Favorite line:</b><br /><br /><i>"Lesson,"Jake said gently. "Man's got the power to break a woman's heart. Women have their own power. Learn this in future, choose better."</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="11430166839663752341" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('zSieZPcaY/kacj0m+7gH5FElsaNIZWuXwOG2dL9giKWMOVMbPjVuQYtkpIwFytcKHp595Eii+7sm6icdhjJU+Q==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('rmdOMUuHeuz4fgs1TWPgYwL/sPAvp7h9zNxgVerYkk7vdoNOgqh3VGlokp+zETCNTUR8ty9gKFEq1/E804pOEg==')})
  }

  <span id="freeText10791030017099466702" style="display:none">Kristen Ashley was born in Gary, Indiana, USA. She nearly killed her mother and herself making it into the world, seeing as she had the umbilical cord wrapped around her neck (already attempting to accessorise and she hadn't taken her first breath!). <br /><br />Kristen grew up in Brownsburg, Indiana but has lived in Denver, Colorado and the West Country of England. Thus she has been blessed to have friends and family around the globe. Her posse is loopy (to say the least) but loopy is good when you want to write.<br /><br />Kristen was raised in a house with a large and multi-generational family. They lived on a very small farm in a small town in the heartland and existed amongst the strains of Glenn Miller, The Everly Brothers, REO Speedwagon and Whitesnake (and the wardrobes that matched).<br /><br />Needless to say, growing up in a house full of music, clothes and love was a good way to grow up. <br /><br />And as she keeps growing up, it keeps getting better.</span>
